                      You now have an opportunity to vacation in the most prestigious community in the Phoenix area. Arrowhead Lakes is one of a handful of Lakefront communities in the desert. This beautiful home is conveniently located near Arrowhead Mall, Desert Ridge, Peoria Sports Complex (Mariner’s Spring Training) and a short drive from Scottsdale. This gem is just 15 minutes from University of Phoenix Stadium... Home of the 2015 Pro Bowl and Superbowl. Enjoy an evening of stiff completion on the black felt of the 7 foot pool table. If you are just unable to leave your work at home. take full advantage of the executive size desk. With the dining table that comfortably seats 8 and additional seating at the granite island, you can enjoy meals with your entire family and a few friends, overlooking the breath-taking view of the lakes and mountains. You are certain to enjoy the resident, ducks, geese, flamingos and occasional boaters. Release the stresses of the day while enjoying a glass of wine in the hot tub, while soaking in the beauty of Arrowhead Lakes. This elegant, quaint, home is one of only a few that has lake views on two sides. With a lake view and patio access, the master bedroom is the perfect setting for romantic evenings and panoramic awakenings. This cozy, home has 3+ bedrooms and sleeps 8. Don’t miss out on this spectacular home. Call soon because it will book fast.

                      <li data-reactid="785"><p data-reactid="786">Leon was wonderful to work with. I noticed a lot of people on here charge extra to use the hot tub, but there was no extra charge for anything. The third guestroom was pretty small, but just fine for our needs. Lots of extra sheets and towels in the linen closet. Wi-Fi, a binder with information about the house and the area, delivery menus, etc. There are several grocery stores and restaurants 5 minutes up the road, big shopping center 10 minutes away, easy mountain hike right behind the subdivision. Lots of wildlife to watch, humming birds, water foul. Saw hot air balloons going over the mountain behind the lake nearly everyday. If you want to be right in the middle of everything, this might not be for you. It's about 20 minutes or so to get to main things in Scottsdale, 30 or so minutes to get downtown Phoenix, 40 minutes or so to the zoo. It is located right by a major freeway so very easy to get anywhere in the metro area. Phoenix is a very drivable city. It was not a problem for us. The only drawback for us was the bed in the master. It was VERY firm. I am used to sleeping on a bed with a foam topper, so I was tossing and turning. This is an easy fix, and if you are interested in staying here but concerned about this, I would just suggest talking to the owner to see if he can make a pillow top available.
